<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:митинг.html>ми́тинг</a> (4820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">meeting</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:митинг.html>ми́тинг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">míting</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:митинг.html>ми́тинга</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:митинг.html>ми́тинги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:митинг.html>ми́тингов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rally, mass-meeting <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a demonstration; an event where people gather together to protest against a given cause or express solidarity</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neologism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> meeting <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">gathering among business people to discuss their business</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:митинговать.html>митингова́ть</a> (20845)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:митинг.html>ми́тинг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">míting</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мишень.html>мише́нь</a> (9654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:мишень.html>мише́нь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mišenĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stamp, round plate, sign, tag</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">nişan</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мишень.html>мише́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mišénʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мишень.html>мише́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мишень.html>мише́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мишень.html>мише́ней</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:младой.html>младо́й</a> (17886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">младъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mladŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*moldъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">young</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молодо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">molodój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***младший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:младший.html>мла́дший</a> (1523)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:младший.html>мла́дший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mládšij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мла́дше</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>younger, youngest (in an earlier period of life)</li>
<li>junior</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:млеть.html>млеть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mletʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

***млечный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:млечный.html>мле́чный</a> (16559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*melčьnъ</i>; synchronically, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мле́ко</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mléko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молочный.html>моло́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">molóčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:млечный.html>мле́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mléčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary or dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> milky</li></ol>

***мнить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мнить.html>мнить</a> (23284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мьнѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mĭněti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мьнити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mĭniti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mьněti</i> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mьniti</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">miñti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to recall, to mention</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">minêt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mention</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέμονα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mémona</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remember</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мнить.html>мнить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mnitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to think, to imagine, to suspect</li></ol>

***многие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:многие.html>многие</a> (637)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>many (people)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:многие.html>мно́гие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говоря́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорый.html>ско́ро</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:война.html>война́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mnógije govorját, što skóro búdet vojná.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Many are saying that soon there will be war.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***много.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> (764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mъnogъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*managas</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*monogʰos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mnógo</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-мно́го" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)бо́льше</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-мно́го" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></b>) <i>(+ genitive case)</i>
</p>
<ol><li>much
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:интересный.html>интере́сного</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mnógo</b> interésnovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">much (of) interest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>many
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mnógo</b> let tomú nazád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">many years ago</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>люде́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mnógo</b> ljudéj prišló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">many people came</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>a lot of, plenty of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выпить.html>вы́пил</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on výpil <b>mnógo</b> vódki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he drank a lot of vodka.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<p>Comparative:
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bóleje</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">more</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<p>Superlative:
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:многодетный.html>многоде́тный</a> (22099)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">много-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mnogo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:многодетный.html>многоде́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mnogodétnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>having many children</li>
<li>large <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">family</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***многое.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:многое.html>мно́гое</a> (1207)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:многое.html>мно́гое</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mnógoje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:многое.html>мно́гого</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the singular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> many things, many a thing, much
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:многое.html>мно́гое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Mnógoje</b> jestʹ što skazátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There is much to tell.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:многое.html>мно́гого</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>жди́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Mnógovo</b> ne ždíte ot nevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don’t expect too much from him.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In origin, this is the neuter singular nominative/accusative of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мно́гий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mnógij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">much, many</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. As an adjective, this is mostly used in the plural. See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мно́гий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mnógij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for the full adjectival declension and more usage examples.
</p>
